The service operates as a gRPC server implementing Envoy's xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) protocol, enabling dynamic configuration delivery to a fleet of proxies without restarts.\n\nThe system is organized around four primary components:\n1. **DiscoveryServer** — the gRPC xDS server managing proxy connections\n2. **ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service)** — bidirectional streaming protocol between Pilot and proxies\n3. **PushContext** — immutable configuration snapshot used during configuration pushes\n4. **ServiceRegistry** — abstraction over service discovery backends (Kubernetes, ServiceEntry, multi-cluster)\n\n---\n\n## 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**Source Files:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`\n\n### Purpose\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is Pilot's core gRPC implementation of Envoy's xDS APIs (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, SDS). It serves as the central hub that:\n- Maintains active connections to all connected Envoy proxies via `adsClients`\n- Coordinates configuration pushes to proxies when Istio resources change\n- Implements request rate limiting and push throttling\n- Manages cache for xDS resources to avoid recomputation\n\n### Key Responsibilities\n\n#### xDS Protocol Implementation\nThe DiscoveryServer implements the Envoy xDS v3 protocol with two operational modes:\n- **Aggregated Discovery Service (ADS)**: A single bidirectional gRPC stream where all resource types (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS) flow over one connection\n- **Delta XDS**: An incremental update protocol for efficient bandwidth usage\n\nThe server registers itself as a gRPC service via the `Register()` method:\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Register(rpcs *grpc.Server) {\n    discovery.RegisterAggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer(rpcs, s)\n}\n```\n\n#### Active Connection Tracking\nThe server maintains a map of active proxy connections:\n```go\nadsClients      map[string]*Connection  // Key: connection ID, Value: active connection\nadsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex            // Protects concurrent access\n```\n\nEach connection represents a long-lived bidirectional stream with an Envoy proxy. When a proxy disconnects, the connection is removed; when new proxies connect, new entries are created.\n\n#### Configuration Push Coordination\nThe push mechanism involves three stages:\n\n1. **Debouncing** (`pushChannel` → `debounce()`)\n   - Configuration change events arrive via `ConfigUpdate()`\n   - Events are buffered in `pushChannel` with configurable debounce timings\n   - Two debounce parameters control the behavior:\n     - `DebounceAfter`: minimum quiet time before triggering a push (e.g., 100ms)\n     - `debounceMax`: maximum time to wait even if events keep arriving (e.g., 10s)\n   - Purpose: prevent thundering herd when multiple config changes arrive in quick succession\n\n2. **Queue Management** (`PushQueue`)\n   - After debouncing, the push request goes to `pushQueue`\n   - The queue merges multiple push requests for the same connection\n   - Connections are processed in order with a semaphore limiting concurrent pushes\n   - Semaphore `concurrentPushLimit` defaults to 100, controlled by `PILOT_PUSH_THROTTLE`\n\n3. **Distribution** (`AdsPushAll()`)\n   - All connected proxies are sent updated configuration\n   - Each proxy's configuration is filtered and customized based on its namespace, labels, and cluster\n   - Push events include a version number for tracking and metric purposes\n\n#### Rate Limiting\nTwo rate limiters protect the server:\n- **Request Rate Limiter** (`RequestRateLimit`): Controls the rate of new xDS requests from proxies (prevents thundering herd during startup)\n- **Push Throttle** (`concurrentPushLimit`): Limits the number of concurrent push operations\n\n### Data Structures\n\n#### DebounceOptions\nControls the timing of configuration pushes:\n```go\ntype DebounceOptions struct {\n    DebounceAfter     time.Duration  // Minimum quiet time (default: features.DebounceAfter)\n    debounceMax       time.Duration  // Maximum wait time (default: features.DebounceMax)\n    enableEDSDebounce bool           // Whether to debounce EDS-only pushes\n}\n```\n\n#### Cache Management\n```go\nCache model.XdsCache  // Stores pre-computed xDS resources (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS)\n```\n\nThe cache stores generated Envoy resources to avoid expensive recomputation for every proxy. It's invalidated when:\n- A full push is triggered: `Cache.ClearAll()`\n- Specific configs are updated: `Cache.Clear(req.ConfigsUpdated)`\n\n### Lifecycle\n\n#### Initialization\n1. `NewDiscoveryServer()` creates the server with empty `adsClients` map\n2. Service generators are registered in the `Generators` map (customization point)\n3. JWT key resolver is initialized for JWT validation\n4. Start parameters: `Start(stopCh)` begins:\n   - `WorkloadEntryController.Run()` for auto-registration\n   - `handleUpdates()` debounce loop\n   - `sendPushes()` queue processor\n   - `Cache.Run()` cache lifecycle management\n   - Periodic metrics refresh\n\n#### Server Readiness\n- `serverReady` flag is set to false initially\n- Set to true only after all caches are synced: `CachesSynced()`\n- Incoming proxy connections are rejected until the flag is true\n- This prevents proxies from receiving incomplete configuration\n\n#### Shutdown\n- `stopCh` signal propagates to all goroutines\n- Active connections are closed gracefully\n- Queue processing stops\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Source Files:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go`\n\n### Purpose\n\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) component handles the gRPC bidirectional stream between a single Envoy proxy and Pilot. It manages:\n- Stream lifecycle (creation, teardown)\n- Request parsing and routing to appropriate xDS generators\n- Push delivery to individual proxies\n- Connection state and proxy metadata\n\n### The Connection Type\n\nThe `Connection` struct wraps the gRPC stream with proxy-specific metadata:\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection                    // Base connection (from go-control-plane)\n    node *core.Node                   // Original Envoy node metadata\n    proxy *model.Proxy                // Pilot's proxy abstraction\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream  // For Delta XDS mode\n    deltaReqChan chan *discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest\n    s *DiscoveryServer               // Reference to parent server\n    ids []string                      // Authenticated identity (SPIFFE)\n}\n```\n\nThe `Proxy` object contains:\n- **Metadata**: cluster ID, network, workload entry, environment variables\n- **Labels**: Kubernetes pod labels used for traffic policies\n- **Namespace**: for RBAC and namespace-scoped resource matching\n- **ID**: unique identifier (pod name + namespace + cluster)\n- **LastPushContext**: the last configuration version this proxy received\n\n### Stream Lifecycle\n\n#### Connection Establishment: `Stream()`\n\nThe `Stream()` function establishes a new bidirectional gRPC stream:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n    // 1. Check server readiness\n    if !s.IsServerReady() {\n        return status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server is not ready\")\n    }\n\n    // 2. Rate limit incoming requests\n    if err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(stream.Context()); err != nil {\n        return status.Errorf(codes.ResourceExhausted, \"request rate limit exceeded\")\n    }\n\n    // 3. Authenticate client (extract SPIFFE identity)\n    ids, err := s.authenticate(ctx)\n\n    // 4. Initialize the push context\n    s.globalPushContext().InitContext(s.Env, nil, nil)\n\n    // 5. Create connection and delegate to xds.Stream\n    con := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n    con.ids = ids\n    con.s = s\n    return xds.Stream(con)\n}\n```\n\n#### Connection Initialization: `initConnection()`\n\nOnce a stream is established, the first DiscoveryRequest arrives with the proxy's node metadata:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) initConnection(node *core.Node, con *Connection, identities []string) error {\n    // 1. Extract proxy metadata from node\n    proxy, err := s.initProxyMetadata(node)\n\n    // 2. Apply cluster aliases if configured\n    if alias, exists := s.ClusterAliases[proxy.Metadata.ClusterID]; exists {\n        proxy.Metadata.ClusterID = alias\n    }\n\n    // 3. Set baseline push context to prevent losing updates\n    proxy.LastPushContext = s.globalPushContext()\n\n    // 4. Assign connection ID and store in adsClients\n    con.SetID(connectionID(proxy.ID))\n    con.proxy = proxy\n    s.addCon(con.ID(), con)\n\n    // 5. Authorize the connection (RBAC check)\n    if err := s.authorize(con, identities); err != nil {\n        return err\n    }\n\n    // 6. Complete proxy initialization (compute initial state)\n    if err := s.initializeProxy(con); err != nil {\n        s.closeConnection(con)\n        return err\n    }\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\nThis initialization ensures:\n- Proxy metadata is extracted and validated\n- RBAC policies are checked (via `s.authorize()`)\n- The proxy state is computed with initial configuration\n- The connection is registered before any concurrent pushes can arrive\n\n#### Connection Teardown: `closeConnection()`\n\nWhen a proxy disconnects (stream ends or client closes):\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) closeConnection(con *Connection) {\n    if con.ID() == \"\" {\n        return  // Not yet initialized\n    }\n    s.removeCon(con.ID())  // Remove from adsClients map\n}\n```\n\n### Request Processing\n\n#### Request Entry Point: `processRequest()`\n\nWhen the proxy sends a DiscoveryRequest:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n    stype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)  // \"cds\", \"lds\", \"rds\", etc.\n\n    // Handle special cases (debug, health check, etc.)\n    if req.TypeUrl == v3.HealthInfoType {\n        return s.handleWorkloadHealthcheck(con.proxy, req)\n    }\n    if strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) {\n        return s.pushXds(con, req.TypeUrl, ...)\n    }\n\n    // Normal processing: delegate to xds.Stream handler\n    // The stream's request processor determines if this is:\n    // - An ACK (nonce matches): no response needed\n    // - A NACK (nonce mismatch): resend the last response\n    // - A new watch: trigger generation and send response\n}\n```\n\nThe request contains:\n- **TypeUrl**: resource type (e.g., \"type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster\")\n- **ResourceNames**: specific resources the proxy wants (e.g., [\"service1\", \"service2\"])\n- **VersionInfo**: version of resources the proxy currently has\n- **ResponseNonce**: token to match responses\n\n#### Watch Management\n\nThe base `xds.Stream` (from go-control-plane) handles:\n- Tracking which resource types each proxy is watching\n- Matching ACKs to responses\n- Detecting retries (NACK on version mismatch)\n- Resource name tracking per connection\n\n### Push Delivery: `pushConnection()`\n\nWhen a configuration push is triggered, each connected proxy receives updates via `pushConnection()`:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) pushConnection(con *Connection, pushEv *Event) error {\n    pushRequest := pushEv.pushRequest\n\n    // 1. For full pushes, compute current proxy state\n    if pushRequest.Full {\n        s.computeProxyState(con.proxy, pushRequest)\n    }\n\n    // 2. Check if this proxy needs any updates\n    pushRequest, needsPush := s.ProxyNeedsPush(con.proxy, pushRequest)\n    if !needsPush {\n        return nil  // Skip push if proxy has latest config\n    }\n\n    // 3. Send updates for each resource type in order\n    // Push order is: CDS → EDS → LDS → RDS → SDS → (others)\n    // This ensures Envoy sees dependencies in correct order\n    wrl := con.watchedResourcesByOrder()\n    for _, w := range wrl {\n        if err := s.pushXds(con, w, pushRequest); err != nil {\n            return err\n        }\n    }\n\n    return nil\n}\n```\n\n**Push Order** is defined to respect Envoy's dependency model:\n1. **CDS** (Cluster Discovery) first — proxies learn about upstream clusters\n2. **EDS** (Endpoint Discovery) — learn which endpoints are in each cluster\n3. **LDS** (Listener Discovery) — configure listeners for traffic\n4. **RDS** (Route Discovery) — configure routes within listeners\n5. **SDS** (Secret Discovery) — TLS certificates\n6. Others (NDS, ECDS, etc.)\n\nThe order prevents Envoy from having incomplete configurations (e.g., routes without listeners).\n\n### Push Queue Management\n\nPushes to individual connections are coordinated via `PushQueue`:\n\n```go\ntype PushQueue struct {\n    pending map[*Connection]*model.PushRequest  // Waiting to be processed\n    queue []*Connection                         // FIFO ordering\n    processing map[*Connection]*model.PushRequest  // Currently being pushed\n}\n```\n\n**Enqueue**: When a push request arrives for a connection:\n- If already pending, the requests are merged (full=true if either is full)\n- If being processed, mark for re-queue after current push completes\n- Add to queue if new\n\n**Dequeue**: Workers process connections FIFO, respecting the semaphore limit:\n- Each `Dequeue()` returns one connection and its merged push request\n- Processing is marked until `MarkDone()` is called\n- If the connection was re-enqueued, it goes back in the queue\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**Source Files:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\n### Purpose\n\nThe `PushContext` is an immutable configuration snapshot created at the start of each push cycle. It aggregates all Istio resources, services, and configuration into a data structure used by xDS generators to produce Envoy configuration.\n\nKey insight: **PushContext is generated once per push**, not once per proxy. All connected proxies use the same PushContext, though generators can customize output per-proxy.\n\n### Responsibilities\n\n1. **Aggregating Configuration**: Collects all relevant Istio resources (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, Sidecars, Gateways, etc.)\n2. **Indexing for Fast Lookup**: Pre-computes indexes to enable O(1) or O(log n) lookups during generation\n3. **Translating Istio Concepts to Envoy**: Converts high-level Istio resources to intermediate representation\n4. **Tracking Push Metrics**: Records success/failure counts for each resource type\n\n### Data Structures\n\n#### Core Configuration Collections\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service discovery results\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex           // All services indexed by hostname, namespace, export level\n\n    // Istio networking policies\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex    // VirtualServices indexed by gateway, namespace\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex  // DestinationRules indexed by namespace\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex                  // Gateways by namespace\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex                  // Sidecar policies\n\n    // Security and policy\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies      // RequestAuthentication, PeerAuthentication\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies       // AuthorizationPolicy\n\n    // Extension points\n    EnvoyFilters envoyFiltersByNamespace       // Patches to Envoy config\n    WasmPlugins wasmPluginsByNamespace         // WebAssembly module injection\n    Telemetry *Telemetries                     // Telemetry policies\n\n    // Mesh-wide configuration\n    Mesh *meshconfig.MeshConfig                // Global mesh configuration\n    Networks *meshconfig.MeshNetworks          // Multi-cluster network topology\n\n    // Caching and state\n    JwtKeyResolver *JwksResolver               // JWKS key resolver\n    NetworkManager *NetworkManager             // Network topology information\n\n    // Metrics\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus  // Push results by error code\n}\n```\n\n#### Service Index\n\nThe `serviceIndex` enables efficient service lookups:\n\n```go\ntype serviceIndex struct {\n    // Services visible across namespaces (exportTo: \"*\")\n    public []*Service\n\n    // Namespace-specific services (exportTo: \".\")\n    privateByNamespace map[string][]*Service\n\n    // Services explicitly exported to specific namespaces\n    exportedToNamespace map[string][]*Service\n\n    // Fast lookup: hostname → namespace → service\n    HostnameAndNamespace map[host.Name]map[string]*Service\n\n    // Pre-cached endpoints grouped by service key and port\n    instancesByPort map[string]map[int][]*IstioEndpoint\n}\n```\n\n**Why indexing matters**: During RDS (route) generation, a proxy may request all services; the index allows O(1) lookups rather than O(n) scans.\n\n#### Virtual Service Index\n\n```go\ntype virtualServiceIndex struct {\n    // VS public to all namespaces, indexed by gateway\n    publicByGateway map[string][]config.Config\n\n    // VS scoped to namespaces, indexed by namespace+gateway\n    privateByNamespaceAndGateway map[types.NamespacedName][]config.Config\n\n    // VS delegation chain: root VS → delegate VS references\n    delegates map[ConfigKey][]ConfigKey\n}\n```\n\n**Use case**: When a proxy in namespace \"default\" requests \"api.default.svc.cluster.local\", the generator queries `HostnameAndNamespace[\"api.default.svc.cluster.local\"][\"default\"]` and finds the matching VirtualService in milliseconds.\n\n#### Destination Rule Index\n\n```go\ntype destinationRuleIndex struct {\n    // DRs by namespace (organized by service)\n    namespaceLocal map[string]*consolidatedDestRules\n\n    // DRs exported by namespaces to others\n    exportedByNamespace map[string]*consolidatedDestRules\n\n    // DRs in root namespace (apply mesh-wide if no local override)\n    rootNamespaceLocal *consolidatedDestRules\n}\n```\n\n**Consolidation**: Multiple DestinationRules for the same service are merged into a single `ConsolidatedDestRule`.\n\n### Initialization: `InitContext()`\n\n`InitContext()` is called once per push to populate the PushContext:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) {\n    ps.initializeMutex.Lock()\n    defer ps.initializeMutex.Unlock()\n\n    // Idempotent: return immediately if already initialized\n    if ps.InitDone.Load() {\n        return\n    }\n\n    // Populate mesh config\n    ps.Mesh = env.Mesh()\n    ps.Networks = env.MeshNetworks()\n\n    // Initialize visibility/export defaults\n    ps.initDefaultExportMaps()\n\n    // Either create new context or incrementally update from old\n    if shouldCreateNew(oldPushContext, pushReq) {\n        ps.createNewContext(env)\n    } else {\n        ps.updateContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq)\n    }\n\n    ps.InitDone.Store(true)\n}\n```\n\n#### Full Context Creation: `createNewContext()`\n\nWhen triggered by full push (e.g., server restart, mesh-wide config change):\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) createNewContext(env *Environment) {\n    ps.initServiceRegistry(env, nil)      // Rebuild service list\n    ps.initKubernetesGateways(env)        // K8s Ingress → Istio Gateway\n    ps.initVirtualServices(env)           // Index all VirtualServices\n    ps.initDestinationRules(env)          // Index all DestinationRules\n    ps.initAuthnPolicies(env)             // Index security policies\n    ps.initAuthorizationPolicies(env)     // Index RBAC policies\n    ps.initTelemetry(env)                 // Index telemetry configs\n    ps.initWasmPlugins(env)               // Index WASM plugins\n    ps.initEnvoyFilters(env, nil, nil)    // Index filter patches\n    ps.initGateways(env)                  // Index Gateways\n    ps.initAmbient(env)                   // Index Ambient mode resources\n    ps.initSidecarScopes(env)             // Index Sidecars (last, depends on others)\n}\n```\n\n**Order matters**: Sidecar scopes are initialized last because they depend on services, VirtualServices, and DestinationRules being available.\n\n#### Incremental Context Update: `updateContext()`\n\nFor partial pushes (e.g., single ServiceEntry added), only changed resources are re-indexed:\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) updateContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest) {\n    // Check which resource types changed\n    for conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n        switch conf.Kind {\n        case kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DNSName:\n            servicesChanged = true\n        case kind.VirtualService:\n            virtualServicesChanged = true\n        case kind.DestinationRule:\n            destinationRulesChanged = true\n        // ... other types\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Reinitialize only changed indexes\n    if servicesChanged {\n        ps.initServiceRegistry(env, pushReq.ConfigsUpdated)\n    } else {\n        ps.ServiceIndex = oldPushContext.ServiceIndex  // Copy unchanged index\n    }\n\n    if virtualServicesChanged {\n        ps.initVirtualServices(env)\n    } else {\n        ps.virtualServiceIndex = oldPushContext.virtualServiceIndex\n    }\n\n    // ... similar for other indexes\n}\n```\n\n### Configuration Translation\n\nThe PushContext doesn't directly generate Envoy resources. Instead, **generators** read from PushContext and produce Envoy protobuf configs:\n\n#### Service → Cluster (CDS)\n\nWhen generating Clusters, the `cds` generator reads:\n- `PushContext.ServiceIndex` to find the service\n- `PushContext.destinationRuleIndex` to find load balancing policy\n- `PushContext.AuthzPolicies` for authorization context\n\nExample lookup flow:\n```\nRequest: \"Generate CDS for proxy in namespace 'default'\"\n1. Query: ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[\"api.default.svc.cluster.local\"][\"default\"]\n2. Get Service object with endpoints, ports\n3. Query: ps.destinationRuleIndex for \"api\" in \"default\"\n4. Merge load balancing policy (round-robin, consistent-hash, etc.)\n5. Generate Envoy Cluster protobuf with Endpoints (EDS)\n```\n\n#### VirtualService → Route (RDS)\n\nWhen generating Routes, the `rds` generator reads:\n- `PushContext.virtualServiceIndex` to find VirtualService\n- Route destinations reference services in PushContext\n- `PushContext.EnvoyFilters` may patch the generated route\n\nExample:\n```\nRequest: \"Generate RDS for proxy in gateway 'istio-system/my-gateway'\"\n1. Query: ps.virtualServiceIndex.publicByGateway[\"istio-system/my-gateway\"]\n2. For each VirtualService:\n   - Extract http/tcp routes\n   - Resolve destination.host to cluster names\n   - Build Envoy RouteConfiguration\n3. Apply EnvoyFilters for patches\n```\n\n#### DestinationRule → Cluster Subset (CDS)\n\nDestinationRules define subsets of endpoints (e.g., \"v1\", \"v2\" versions):\n\n```\nDestinationRule:\n  spec:\n    subsets:\n    - name: v1\n      labels:\n        version: v1\n    - name: v2\n      labels:\n        version: v2\n```\n\nCDS generator creates separate Cluster for each subset:\n- `api-v1` cluster: endpoints with label `version=v1`\n- `api-v2` cluster: endpoints with label `version=v2`\n\nQueries PushContext:\n- `ps.destinationRuleIndex` for the DestinationRule\n- `ps.ServiceIndex.instancesByPort` for labeled endpoints\n\n### Push Metrics and Error Tracking\n\nPushContext tracks push statistics:\n\n```go\ntype ProxyPushStatus struct {\n    PushStartTime      int64\n    PushDuration       int64  // milliseconds\n    Err                string\n    // ... per-type status\n}\n```\n\nCaptured during push:\n- Successful resource generation\n- Errors (missing services, invalid config, etc.)\n- Per-proxy metrics for debugging\n\n### Relationship to Service Registry\n\nPushContext reads from the service registry via `env.ServiceRegistry()` and `env.GetServices()`:\n- **Services** come from: Kubernetes Services + ServiceEntry resources\n- **Endpoints** come from: Kubernetes Endpoints/EndpointSlice + ServiceEntry\n- **Service Accounts** come from: Kubernetes Pods + manual service account mapping\n\nPush trigger flow:\n```\nService Registry Event (e.g., pod added)\n↓\nConfigUpdate() → pushChannel\n↓\ndebounce (100ms - 10s)\n↓\nPush() → initPushContext() → new PushContext\n↓\nPushContext.initServiceRegistry() queries registry\n↓\nGenerators use PushContext.ServiceIndex\n↓\nxDS resources generated and sent to proxies\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Source Files:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/`, `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/`\n\n### Purpose\n\nThe Service Registry abstracts away the underlying service discovery source. Pilot can aggregate services from:\n- **Kubernetes**: Services, Endpoints, Pods\n- **Service Entries**: Manual service definitions\n- **Multi-cluster**: Services from remote clusters\n- **VMs**: WorkloadEntry resources for VMs outside Kubernetes\n\n### ServiceRegistry Interface\n\n```go\ntype Instance interface {\n    model.Controller                // Event handlers: AppendServiceHandler, Run()\n    model.ServiceDiscovery          // Query methods: GetServices(), InstancesByPort(), etc.\n    Provider() provider.ID          // \"kubernetes\", \"workload\", etc.\n    Cluster() cluster.ID            // Cluster ID for multi-cluster\n}\n```\n\n**Controller** provides event-driven notifications:\n- `AppendServiceHandler(f ServiceHandler)` — register callback for service changes\n- `Run(stop <-chan struct{})` — start the controller\n\n**ServiceDiscovery** provides query interface:\n- `GetServices()` — list all services\n- `GetService(hostname)` — lookup specific service\n- `InstancesByPort(service, port, labels)` — find endpoints for a service\n\n### Kubernetes Service Registry Implementation\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go`\n\nThe Kubernetes controller watches:\n\n```go\ntype Controller struct {\n    // Watched Kubernetes resources\n    namespaces kclient.Client[*v1.Namespace]    // Watch namespaces\n    services   kclient.Client[*v1.Service]      // Watch k8s Services\n    endpoints *endpointSliceController          // Watch EndpointSlices\n    nodes     kclient.Client[*v1.Node]          // Watch nodes (for gateway addresses)\n    pods      *PodCache                         // Watch Pods (for endpoints, RBAC)\n\n    // Conversion to Istio model\n    servicesMap map[host.Name]*model.Service   // Kubernetes Service → Istio Service\n    nodeInfoMap map[string]kubernetesNode      // Node info for NodePort IPs\n\n    // Event handlers\n    handlers model.ControllerHandlers            // Registered handlers from PushContext\n}\n```\n\n#### Service Discovery Flow\n\n**1. Service Watch**\n\nWhen a Kubernetes Service is created:\n```\nK8s Event: Service \"api\" in namespace \"default\"\n↓\nController.onServiceUpdate()\n↓\nConverts: v1.Service → model.Service\n  - Extract name, namespace, ports, labels, selectors\n  - Create hostname: \"api.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n↓\nUpdates: Controller.servicesMap[\"api.default.svc.cluster.local\"]\n↓\nFires: ServiceHandler callbacks\n```\n\n**2. Endpoint Discovery**\n\nWhen pods are added/removed, EndpointSlices are updated:\n```\nK8s Event: EndpointSlice updated (new pod ready)\n↓\nController.onEndpointUpdate()\n↓\nQueries: Pod cache for pod metadata (labels, node, IP)\n↓\nResolves: K8s Service selector → matching pods\n↓\nCreates: model.IstioEndpoint entries (IP, port, labels, zone, ...)\n↓\nFires: ServiceHandler with updated service\n```\n\n**3. Push Trigger**\n\nService change triggers configuration push:\n```go\nfunc (c *Controller) onServiceUpdate(oldSvc, newSvc *v1.Service, event model.Event) {\n    // Determine what changed (ports, labels, selectors, etc.)\n\n    // Trigger push for affected services\n    c.opts.XDSUpdater.ConfigUpdate(&model.PushRequest{\n        Full: true,  // or false for EDS-only push\n        ConfigsUpdated: map[model.ConfigKey]bool{\n            {Kind: kind.Service, Name: \"api\", Namespace: \"default\"}: true,\n        },\n        Reason: model.NewReasonStats(model.ServiceUpdate),\n    })\n}\n```\n\n#### CDS vs. EDS Push\n\nService changes can trigger different push types:\n\n**Full Push (CDS + LDS + RDS + EDS)**:\n- Service ports changed (requires new Envoy Clusters)\n- Service selectors changed (different endpoints)\n- Service labels changed (affects traffic policies)\n- Service visibility changed (exportTo)\n\n**EDS-Only Push**:\n- Pod scaled up/down (new endpoint IP, same service definition)\n- Pod health changed (endpoint removed from available set)\n- Pod labels changed (subset routing affected)\n\nEDS is much lighter weight than full push:\n- No new Cluster generation\n- No new Route generation\n- Just update endpoint list in existing Cluster\n\n### Multi-Cluster Service Aggregation\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/multicluster.go`, `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/`\n\nIn multi-cluster deployments, Pilot aggregates services from multiple clusters:\n\n```\nCluster A: K8s Controller\n    └─ Services: api.default, web.default\n       Endpoints: [10.0.1.2:8080, 10.0.1.3:8080]\n\nCluster B: K8s Controller\n    └─ Services: api.default, web.default\n       Endpoints: [10.0.2.2:8080, 10.0.2.3:8080]\n\n       ↓ (via ServiceExport/ServiceImport or Istio ServiceEntry)\n\nAggregate Controller:\n    └─ api.default: [10.0.1.2, 10.0.1.3, 10.0.2.2, 10.0.2.3]\n       (with cluster labels on each endpoint)\n```\n\n#### Multi-Cluster Modes\n\n**1. Shared Control Plane (Pilot runs in Cluster A)**\n- Pilot watches Kubernetes in Cluster A and reads remote Cluster B via API server or agent\n- Uses `MeshNetworks` config to route traffic across clusters\n- Endpoints are labeled with cluster: \"A\" or \"B\"\n- Gateway pods in Cluster B handle cross-cluster ingress\n\n**2. Shared Network**\n- All pods on same network (no NAT)\n- Proxies directly reach endpoints in remote clusters\n- Endpoints include ClusterName label for debugging\n\n**3. Cross-Network**\n- Each cluster on separate network (NAT)\n- Ingress gateway in remote cluster exposes services\n- Endpoints point to gateway IP:port instead of pod IPs\n\n#### ServiceExport and ServiceImport\n\nKubernetes ServiceExport/ServiceImport resources control multi-cluster visibility:\n\n```yaml\n# Cluster A\napiVersion: net.gke.io/v1\nkind: ServiceExport\nmetadata:\n  name: api\n  namespace: default\n---\n# Cluster B (MCS controller syncs ServiceExport)\napiVersion: net.gke.io/v1\nkind: ServiceImport\nmetadata:\n  name: api\n  namespace: default\nspec:\n  ports:\n  - port: 8080\n  ips:\n  - 10.0.1.1  # Ingress gateway IP in Cluster A\n```\n\n### Workload Entries and Auto-Registration\n\n**Purpose**: Support VMs and non-Kubernetes workloads in the Istio mesh\n\n**Source:** `pilot/pkg/autoregistration/`\n\nWorkloadEntry resources define VMs:\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: WorkloadEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: vm-api-1\nspec:\n  address: 192.168.1.10\n  ports:\n    http: 8080\n  labels:\n    app: api\n    version: v1\n```\n\nWorkloadEntry → Service flow:\n1. Pilot's workload controller watches WorkloadEntry CRD\n2. Creates `model.IstioEndpoint` for the VM\n3. Associates it with a Service (via matching label selectors)\n4. Includes in EDS response to proxies\n\nAuto-registration (for non-Kubernetes proxies):\n- Proxy connects to Pilot with metadata (VM IP, port, labels)\n- Pilot auto-creates WorkloadEntry\n- Subsequently treated like any other endpoint\n\n### Dependency Between Registry and DiscoveryServer\n\nThe push flow connects service changes to xDS updates:\n\n```\nService Registry        PushContext         DiscoveryServer        Proxies\n(K8s, ServiceEntry)\n        │\n        ├─ ServiceHandler fired\n        │       │\n        │       └─ ConfigUpdate(pushRequest)\n        │               │\n        │               ├─ pushChannel (debounce)\n        │               │\n        │               └─ Push()\n        │                   │\n        │                   ├─ initPushContext()\n        │                   │   └─ ServiceRegistry.GetServices()  ← New query\n        │                   │\n        │                   └─ AdsPushAll()\n        │                       └─ pushConnection()\n        │                           └─ pushXds() (CDS, EDS, LDS, RDS)\n        │                               └─ Send to proxy\n        └─────────────────────────────────────────────→\n```\n\n**Key point**: Every service change query the registry fresh (via `InitContext` → `initServiceRegistry`). PushContext doesn't cache service data across pushes.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Data Flow: Configuration Change to xDS Push\n\n### End-to-End Example: Adding a Pod\n\n```\n1. Kubernetes Event: Pod \"api-v2-xyz\" created\n   - Ready status: Running\n   - IP: 10.0.1.5\n   - Labels: app=api, version=v2\n   - Service selector match: app=api\n\n2. Kube Controller Detects Change\n   - Watch fires for EndpointSlice\n   - Queries Pod cache for pod metadata\n   - Creates IstioEndpoint for 10.0.1.5:8080\n\n3. Push Trigger\n   - ServiceHandler callback from kube controller\n   - Calls ConfigUpdate() with reason: model.ServiceUpdate\n   - Push request goes to pushChannel\n\n4. Debounce\n   - Default: wait 100ms after last change\n   - Max: 10 seconds absolute\n   - If no new changes in 100ms, proceed to push\n\n5. PushContext Initialization\n   - initPushContext() called by Push()\n   - PushContext.initServiceRegistry() queries registry\n   - ServiceIndex rebuilt with new endpoint\n   - Lookup: ps.ServiceIndex[\"api.default\"][8080] → includes 10.0.1.5\n\n6. xDS Generation\n   - For each connected proxy:\n     - Call pushConnection() with PushContext\n     - CDS generator: checks if proxy needs cluster \"api\" (yes)\n     - EDS generator: loads endpoints from PushContext.ServiceIndex\n     - Generates EDS update with [10.0.1.2, 10.0.1.3, 10.0.1.5]\n     - Send: DiscoveryResponse with new EDS version\n\n7. Proxy Update\n   - Envoy proxy receives EDS response\n   - Adds 10.0.1.5 to connection pool\n   - Starts health checking\n   - Traffic gradually shifts to new endpoint\n```\n\n### Example: Applying VirtualService\n\n```\n1. Istio Event: VirtualService \"api\" created\n   kubectl apply -f virtualservice.yaml\n\n2. Config Watcher Detects Change\n   - ConfigStore watches VirtualService CRD\n   - Fires ConfigUpdate() with reason: model.ConfigChange\n   - ConfigsUpdated: {Kind: VirtualService, Name: \"api\", Namespace: \"default\"}\n\n3. Push Trigger\n   - pushChannel receives PushRequest\n   - Debounce waits for stability\n   - Push() called\n\n4. PushContext Initialization\n   - initPushContext() called\n   - updateContext() detects virtualServicesChanged = true\n   - initVirtualServices() re-indexes all VS\n   - virtualServiceIndex rebuilt with new VS\n\n5. xDS Generation\n   - For each connected proxy:\n     - Determine which proxies care about \"api\" VS\n       - Proxy in gateway namespace: yes\n       - Proxy in other namespace with exportTo: yes\n       - Proxy in private namespace: only if vs.exportTo includes it\n     - RDS generator:\n       - Looks up vs in virtualServiceIndex\n       - Extracts routes from vs.http[]/tcp[]\n       - For each route destination, resolve service to cluster name\n       - Generate Envoy RouteConfiguration\n     - LDS generator:\n       - May need new listener if vs.hosts changed significantly\n     - Send: DiscoveryResponse with new RDS/LDS versions\n\n6. Proxy Update\n   - Envoy receives RDS with new routes\n   - Traffic to \"api\" now respects defined routes\n   - Headers, timeouts, retries applied\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Extension Points\n\n### 1. Custom xDS Generators\n\n**How**: Register in `DiscoveryServer.Generators` map\n\n**Why**: Customize resource generation per client type\n\n**Example**: Different configuration for different Envoy versions or proxy types\n\n```go\ngenerators := map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator{\n    \"envoy-v1\": &CustomGeneratorV1{},\n    \"envoy-v2\": &CustomGeneratorV2{},\n}\ndiscoveryServer.Generators = generators\n```\n\nGenerators implement:\n```go\ntype XdsResourceGenerator interface {\n    Generate(proxy *Proxy, push *PushContext,\n             req *model.PushRequest, w *model.WatchedResource) model.Resources\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Custom ProxyNeedsPush Filter\n\n**How**: Set `DiscoveryServer.ProxyNeedsPush` function\n\n**Why**: Skip pushes for certain proxies (e.g., workload-specific pushes)\n\n```go\ndiscoveryServer.ProxyNeedsPush = func(proxy *Proxy, req *PushRequest) (*PushRequest, bool) {\n    // Return true to send push, false to skip\n    if !proxyInterested(proxy, req) {\n        return nil, false\n    }\n    return req, true\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Custom Service Discovery Backend\n\n**How**: Implement `serviceregistry.Instance` interface and register\n\n**Why**: Add non-Kubernetes sources (Consul, Cloud Run, custom registry)\n\n```go\ntype CustomRegistry struct {}\n\nfunc (cr *CustomRegistry) GetServices() []*model.Service {\n    // Query custom backend\n}\n\nfunc (cr *CustomRegistry) Provider() provider.ID {\n    return \"custom\"\n}\n\n// Register with Pilot\nenv.ServiceRegistry().RegisterRegistry(customRegistry)\n```\n\n### 4. EnvoyFilter Patches\n\n**How**: Apply EnvoyFilter resources\n\n**Why**: Modify generated Envoy config without changing core generators\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: EnvoyFilter\nmetadata:\n  name: custom-filter\nspec:\n  workloadSelector:\n    labels:\n      app: api\n  configPatches:\n  - applyTo: CLUSTER\n    patch:\n      operation: MERGE\n      value:\n        outlierDetection:\n          consecutive5xx: 5\n```\n\n### 5. WASM Plugin Injection\n\n**How**: Create WasmPlugin resource\n\n**Why**: Inject custom WASM modules into proxy initialization\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: extensions.istio.io/v1alpha1\nkind: WasmPlugin\nmetadata:\n  name: auth-filter\nspec:\n  selector:\n    matchLabels:\n      app: api\n  url: oci://myregistry.com/auth-filter:v1.0\n  phase: AUTHN\n  config: |\n    {\n      \"iss\": \"https://auth.example.com\"\n    }\n```\n\n### 6. Custom Event Handlers\n\n**How**: Implement `model.ServiceHandler` and append to controller\n\n**Why**: React to service changes (custom logging, metrics, external integrations)\n\n```go\ncontroller.AppendServiceHandler(func(old, new *model.Service, event model.Event) {\n    // React to service changes\n    if event == model.EventAdd {\n        log.Infof(\"New service: %s\", new.Hostname)\n    }\n})\n```\n\n### 7. Telemetry and Metrics Plugins\n\n**How**: Implement telemetry generation callbacks\n\n**Why**: Emit custom metrics, logs, or traces\n\n- `PushRequest.Reason` — tracks push trigger reason\n- `PushContext.ProxyStatus` — records per-proxy push results\n- Metrics hooks in push flow for custom instrumentation\n\n---\n\n## 7. Error Handling\n\n### Configuration Validation Errors\n\n**Source**: `push_context.go` — during initialization\n\n**Handling**:\n1. Validator checks config before adding to PushContext\n2. Invalid configs are logged but don't block entire push\n3. Affected proxies marked in `ProxyStatus[error][proxyID]`\n4. Other proxies still get valid config\n\n**Example**: Invalid DestinationRule syntax\n```\nError: \"DestinationRule api: invalid subset labels\"\nAction: Log error, skip this DestinationRule, continue\nResult: Proxies get config without this DestinationRule\n```\n\n### Push Failures\n\n**Source**: `ads.go` — during `pushConnection()`\n\n**Scenarios**:\n1. **Generator returns error** — skip that resource type, log error\n2. **Network error sending response** — connection closes, proxy reconnects\n3. **Out of memory** — graceful degradation, skip some proxies\n\n**Handling**:\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) pushXds(con *Connection, w string, req *model.PushRequest) error {\n    res, err := s.generate(con.proxy, req, w)\n    if err != nil {\n        log.Errorf(\"Generate error for %v type %s: %v\", con.ID(), w, err)\n        return err  // Connection closed\n    }\n    // Send response...\n}\n```\n\n### Service Registry Errors\n\n**Source**: Kube controller, custom registry implementations\n\n**Scenarios**:\n1. **API server down** — controller queues events, retries\n2. **Label selector syntax invalid** — error logged, service skipped\n3. **Endpoint data incomplete** — partial data included, warning logged\n\n**Handling**:\n- Endpoints without pod metadata: included with empty labels\n- Missing services: DestinationRule rules ignored (no matching service)\n- Registry desync: Full push triggered to resync\n\n### Proxy Disconnection\n\n**Source**: `ads.go` — stream closed\n\n**Handling**:\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) closeConnection(con *Connection) {\n    s.removeCon(con.ID())  // Remove from adsClients\n    // Resources allocated by this connection are freed\n    // Pushed queued to this proxy are discarded\n}\n```\n\nProxy can:\n- Reconnect immediately (gRPC reconnect)\n- Reconnect after backoff\n- Or fail and require restart\n\n---\n\n## 8. Key Concepts and Terminology\n\n### Push\nA push event where the DiscoveryServer sends updated xDS resources to one or all connected proxies. Triggered by configuration changes in Istio resources or service registry.\n\n### Full Push\nA push where all xDS resource types are generated fresh. Triggered by mesh-wide configuration changes or explicit requests.\n\n### Incremental Push / EDS Push\nA push where only Endpoint Discovery Service is updated. Triggered by service endpoint changes (pod scaling, health status).\n\n### PushVersion\nA unique version identifier for each push cycle. Included in xDS responses. Used by proxies to identify stale configurations.\n\n### Watch\nA proxy's interest in a specific xDS resource type. Established via DiscoveryRequest with a TypeUrl. Tracked per connection.\n\n### Nonce\nA token in xDS requests/responses used to match ACKs (acknowledgments) to responses. Ensures correct state synchronization.\n\n### Connection ID\nA unique identifier for a proxy's connection to Pilot. Format: `pod-name.namespace.cluster-id`. Used to track connected proxies.\n\n### Resource Name\nIn xDS, the specific resource being requested. Examples:\n- Cluster: \"api.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n- Route: \"http.80\"\n- Listener: \"0.0.0.0_8080\"\n\n### Visibility / ExportTo\nKubernetes namespace export control. Determines which namespaces can see a service or VirtualService.\n- `\".\"` — same namespace only\n- `\"*\"` — all namespaces\n- `\"namespace\"` — specific namespace\n\n### Subset\nA subset of endpoints for a service, defined via DestinationRule. Enables routing to specific versions (e.g., \"v1\", \"v2\").\n\n---\n\n## 9. Relevant Source Files Reference\n\n### Core Discovery Server\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` — DiscoveryServer struct, push coordination, debounce\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` — ADS implementation, Stream, Connection, processRequest, pushConnection\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go` — Delta/incremental xDS implementation\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go` — Queue for ordered push processing\n\n### Resource Generators\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` — Cluster Discovery Service (Envoy clusters)\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` — Listener Discovery Service (Envoy listeners)\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` — Route Discovery Service (Envoy routes)\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` — Endpoint Discovery Service (Envoy endpoints)\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/sds.go` — Secret Discovery Service (TLS certificates)\n\n### Configuration Snapshots\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` — PushContext structure, indexing, initialization\n- `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` — Service and Port definitions\n- `pilot/pkg/model/virtualservice.go` — VirtualService model\n- `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` — DestinationRule model\n\n### Service Discovery\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/instance.go` — ServiceRegistry interface\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/controller.go` — Kubernetes controller\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/endpointslice.go` — Endpoint synchronization\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller/multicluster.go` — Multi-cluster aggregation\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/` — Service aggregation across registries\n\n### Environment and Context\n- `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` — Environment and global state\n- `pilot/pkg/model/config.go` — Configuration resource types\n\n---\n\n## 10. Summary: The Complete Picture\n\nIstio Pilot's Discovery Service is a sophisticated configuration distribution system built around these principles:\n\n1. **Event-Driven**: Service changes (pods, configs) trigger pushes asynchronously\n2. **Debounced**: Multiple changes within milliseconds are merged into single push\n3. **Ordered**: xDS resources are sent in dependency order (CDS → EDS → LDS → RDS)\n4. **Cached**: Pre-computed resources and indexes avoid recomputation\n5. **Scalable**: Separate threads for debouncing, queuing, and per-proxy push\n6. **Extensible**: Custom generators, filters, and backends can be plugged in\n\nThe flow from configuration change to proxy update:\n```\nConfig Change (K8s, ServiceEntry, VirtualService)\n    ↓\nServiceRegistry Event Handler\n    ↓\nConfigUpdate() → pushChannel\n    ↓\ndebounce() — wait for stability\n    ↓\nPush() — create PushContext with fresh config\n    ↓\ninitPushContext() → rebuild indexes from registry\n    ↓\nAdsPushAll() → queue connections for push\n    ↓\nsendPushes() — dequeue connections\n    ↓\npushConnection() → generate and send xDS per proxy\n    ↓\nEnvoy Proxy receives DiscoveryResponse\n    ↓\nUpdates configuration and re-routes traffic\n```\n\nThis architecture enables Istio to manage complex, dynamic service meshes with thousands of proxies while maintaining configuration consistency and responsiveness.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
